					else_if = {	limit = { NOT = { exists = event_target:s_c10_06_012 } } save_global_event_target_as = s_c10_06_012 }
					else_if = {	limit = { NOT = { exists = event_target:s_c10_06_013 } } save_global_event_target_as = s_c10_06_013 }
					else_if = {	limit = { NOT = { exists = event_target:s_c10_06_014 } } save_global_event_target_as = s_c10_06_014 }
					else_if = {	limit = { NOT = { exists = event_target:s_c10_06_015 } } save_global_event_target_as = s_c10_06_015 }
				}
			}
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = { is_country_type = global_event }
			log = "--------------------------------------------------"
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_binary value > 0 } }			log = "              Binary: [this.mapping_binary]" }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_trinary value > 0 } }			log = "              Trinary: [this.mapping_trinary]" }
			log = "--------------------------------------------------"
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_stellar_remnants value > 0 } }	log = "              Stellar Remnant: [this.mapping_stellar_remnants]" }
			log = "-------------------------"
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_sc_black_hole value > 0 } }		log = "              Black Holes: [this.mapping_sc_black_hole]" }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_sc_d value > 0 } }				log = "              Class D Stars: [this.mapping_sc_d]" }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_sc_neutron_star value > 0 } }	log = "              Neutron Stars: [this.mapping_sc_neutron_star]" }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_sc_pulsar value > 0 } }			log = "              Pulsars: [this.mapping_sc_pulsar]" }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_sc_nova value > 0 } }			log = "              Novas: [this.mapping_sc_nova]" }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_sc_collapsar value > 0 } }		log = "              Collapsers: [this.mapping_sc_collapsar]" }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_sc_p value > 0 } }				log = "              Planetary Nebulas: [this.mapping_sc_p]" }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_sc_magnetar value > 0 } }		log = "              Magnetars: [this.mapping_sc_magnetar]" }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_sc_microquasar value > 0 } }	log = "              Microquasars: [this.mapping_sc_microquasar]" }
			log = "--------------------------------------------------"
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_giant_stars value > 0 } }		log = "              Giant Star: [this.mapping_giant_stars]" }
			log = "-------------------------"
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_giant_sc_o value > 0 } }		log = "              Class O Stars: [this.mapping_giant_sc_o]" }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_giant_sc_b value > 0 } }		log = "              Class B Stars: [this.mapping_giant_sc_b]" }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_giant_sc_f value > 0 } }		log = "              Class F Stars: [this.mapping_giant_sc_f]" }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_giant_sc_g value > 0 } }		log = "              Class G Stars: [this.mapping_giant_sc_g]" }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_giant_sc_k value > 0 } }		log = "              Class K Stars: [this.mapping_giant_sc_k]" }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_giant_sc_m value > 0 } }		log = "              Class M Stars: [this.mapping_giant_sc_m]" }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_giant_sc_w value > 0 } }		log = "              Class W Stars: [this.mapping_giant_sc_w]" }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_giant_sc_c value > 0 } }		log = "              Class C Stars: [this.mapping_giant_sc_c]" }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_giant_sc_s value > 0 } }		log = "              Class S Stars: [this.mapping_giant_sc_s]" }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_giant_sc_a value > 0 } }		log = "              Class A Stars: [this.mapping_giant_sc_a]" }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_giant_sc_lbv value > 0 } }		log = "              Luminous Stars: [this.mapping_giant_sc_lbv]" }
			log = "--------------------------------------------------"
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_fledgling_stars value > 0 } }	log = "              Fledgling: [this.mapping_fledgling_stars]" }
			log = "-------------------------"
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_sc_protostar value > 0 } }		log = "              Protostarss: [this.mapping_sc_protostar]" }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_sc_tt value > 0 } }				log = "              T Tauri Stars: [this.mapping_sc_tt]" }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_sc_a value > 0 } }				log = "              Class A Stars: [this.mapping_sc_a]" }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_sc_ae value > 0 } }				log = "              Herbig Stars: [this.mapping_sc_ae]" }
			log = "--------------------------------------------------"
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_dwarf_stars value > 0 } }		log = "              Dwarf Star: [this.mapping_dwarf_stars]" }
			log = "-------------------------"
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_sc_g value > 0 } }				log = "              Class G Stars: [this.mapping_sc_g]" }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_sc_k value > 0 } }				log = "              Class K Stars: [this.mapping_sc_k]" }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_sc_m value > 0 } }				log = "              Class M Stars: [this.mapping_sc_m]" }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_sc_t value > 0 } }				log = "              Class T Stars: [this.mapping_sc_t]" }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_sc_l value > 0 } }				log = "              Class L Stars: [this.mapping_sc_l]" }
			if = { limit = { check_variable = { which = mapping_sc_y value > 0 } }				log = "              Class Y Stars: [this.mapping_sc_y]" }
			log = "--------------------------------------------------"
		}
	}
}
